LLM generates decomposition with:\\n   - `ideal_agent`: unconstrained best agent\\n   - `ideal_agent_desc`: description of ideal agent's capabilities\\n   - `assigned_agent`: best available from manifest\\n   - `match_quality`: \\\"excellent\\\" | \\\"acceptable\\\" | \\\"insufficient\\\"\\n\\n3. `verify_lite()` validates and routes:\\n   - \\\"insufficient\\\" \\u2192 spawns ad-hoc agent with `is_spawn=True`\\n   - \\\"excellent\\\"/\\\"acceptable\\\" \\u2192 uses `assigned_agent` from manifest\\n\\n### Key Files:\\n- `packages/reasoning/src/aurora_reasoning/prompts/decompose.py:19-90` - Prompt that defines match_quality\\n- `packages/soar/src/aurora_soar/phases/verify.py:19-145` - verify_lite that uses match_quality\\n- `packages/cli/src/aurora_cli/planning/agents.py:357-893` - AgentRecommender (legacy keyword-based)\\n\\n### Current Gaps:\\n1. **No fallback chain**: When `match_quality=insufficient`, it only tries ad-hoc spawn, no fallback hierarchy\\n2. **Binary matching**: `excellent` and `acceptable` treated identically in execution\\n3. **No one-shot examples**: Decomposition prompt lacks few-shot examples of good agent matching\\n4. **No agent capability context**: LLM doesn't see full agent descriptions/capabilities\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Improved Agent Matching Algorithm Design\\n\\n### 1. Enhanced Prompt with One-Shot Examples\\n\\nAdd concrete examples to the decomposition prompt showing good match_quality decisions:\\n\\n```python\\n# In decompose.py build_system_prompt()\\nFEW_SHOT_EXAMPLES = \\\"\\\"\\\"\\nEXAMPLE 1 - Excellent match:\\nTask: \\\"Write unit tests for the payment module\\\"\\nideal_agent: \\\"@qa-test-architect\\\"\\nideal_agent_desc: \\\"Testing and QA specialist\\\"\\nassigned_agent: \\\"@qa-test-architect\\\"\\nmatch_quality: \\\"excellent\\\"\\nReasoning: Testing is @qa-test-architect's core specialty.\\n\\nEXAMPLE 2 - Acceptable match:\\nTask: \\\"Create wireframes for the onboarding flow\\\"\\nideal_agent: \\\"@ux-designer\\\"\\nideal_agent_desc: \\\"UI/UX design specialist\\\"\\nassigned_agent: \\\"@ux-expert\\\"\\nmatch_quality: \\\"acceptable\\\"\\nReasoning: @ux-expert handles UX, though @ux-designer would be more specialized.\\n\\nEXAMPLE 3 - Insufficient match:\\nTask: \\\"Write a compelling marketing story for the product launch\\\"\\nideal_agent: \\\"@creative-writer\\\"\\nideal_agent_desc: \\\"Narrative and creative writing specialist\\\"\\nassigned_agent: \\\"@business-analyst\\\"\\nmatch_quality: \\\"insufficient\\\"\\nReasoning: No creative writing agent exists. @business-analyst can research but lacks narrative expertise.\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### 2. Tiered Fallback Strategy\\n\\nImplement a fallback chain for insufficient matches:\\n\\n```python\\nclass MatchQualityTier(Enum):\\n    EXCELLENT = \\\"excellent\\\"    # Score >= 0.85: Agent's core specialty\\n    ACCEPTABLE = \\\"acceptable\\\"  # Score 0.5-0.84: Capable but not specialized\\n    INSUFFICIENT = \\\"insufficient\\\"  # Score < 0.5: No capable agent\\n\\nclass FallbackStrategy:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Fallback strategies for insufficient matches.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    \\n    FALLBACK_CHAIN = [\\n        # (capability_category, fallback_agents)\\n        (\\\"creative\\\", [\\\"@business-analyst\\\", \\\"@master\\\"]),\\n        (\\\"technical\\\", [\\\"@full-stack-dev\\\", \\\"@holistic-architect\\\"]),\\n        (\\\"analysis\\\", [\\\"@business-analyst\\\", \\\"@product-manager\\\"]),\\n        (\\\"testing\\\", [\\\"@qa-test-architect\\\", \\\"@full-stack-dev\\\"]),\\n        (\\\"design\\\", [\\\"@ux-expert\\\", \\\"@holistic-architect\\\"]),\\n    ]\\n    \\n    @staticmethod\\n    def get_fallback(task_description: str, available_agents: list[str]) -> tuple[str, str]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Get best fallback agent for insufficient match.\\n        \\n        Returns:\\n            (fallback_agent, fallback_reason)\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        # Categorize task\\n        category = _categorize_task(task_description)\\n        \\n        # Find first available fallback\\n        for cat, fallbacks in FallbackStrategy.FALLBACK_CHAIN:\\n            if cat == category:\\n                for agent in fallbacks:\\n                    if agent in available_agents:\\n                        return (agent, f\\\"Fallback for {category} tasks\\\")\\n        \\n        # Ultimate fallback\\n        return (\\\"@master\\\", \\\"General-purpose fallback\\\")\\n```\\n\\n### 3. Enhanced Agent Context in Prompts\\n\\nProvide richer agent context to the LLM:\\n\\n```python\\ndef _format_agents_with_capabilities(available_agents: list) -> str:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Format agents with full capability context for LLM.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    lines = []\\n    for agent in available_agents:\\n        capabilities = getattr(agent, \\\"capabilities\\\", [])\\n        when_to_use = getattr(agent, \\\"when_to_use\\\", \\\"\\\")\\n        \\n        lines.append(f\\\"### @{agent.id}\\\")\\n        if when_to_use:\\n            lines.append(f\\\"Use when: {when_to_use}\\\")\\n        if capabilities:\\n            lines.append(f\\\"Capabilities: {', '.join(capabilities[:5])}\\\")\\n        lines.append(\\\"\\\")\\n    \\n    return \\\"\\\\n\\\".join(lines)\\n```\\n\\n### 4. Quality-Aware Execution Routing\\n\\nDifferent execution paths based on match quality:\\n\\n```python\\ndef execute_with_quality_awareness(\\n    subgoal: dict,\\n    agent_assignments: list,\\n    match_quality: str,\\n) -> ExecutionResult:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Route execution based on match quality tier.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    \\n    if match_quality == \\\"excellent\\\":\\n        # Direct execution with full confidence\\n        return execute_agent(agent_assignments[0])\\n    \\n    elif match_quality == \\\"acceptable\\\":\\n        # Execute with confidence boost request\\n        return execute_agent(\\n            agent_assignments[0],\\n            prompt_suffix=\\\"Note: You're handling a task outside your core specialty. \\\"\\n                          \\\"Be thorough and highlight any areas where specialized expertise might help.\\\"\\n        )\\n    \\n    elif match_quality == \\\"insufficient\\\":\\n        # Try spawn first, then fallback chain\\n        try:\\n            return spawn_adhoc_agent(subgoal)\\n        except SpawnError:\\n            fallback_agent, reason = FallbackStrategy.get_fallback(\\n                subgoal[\\\"description\\\"],\\n                available_agents\\n            )\\n            return execute_agent(\\n                fallback_agent,\\n                prompt_suffix=f\\\"Note: {reason}. Identify gaps in your analysis.\\\"\\n            )\\n```\\n\\n### 5. Match Quality Validation in verify_lite\\n\\nEnhance verify_lite to validate and potentially adjust match_quality:\\n\\n```python\\ndef verify_lite_enhanced(\\n    decomposition: dict,\\n    available_agents: list,\\n) -> tuple[bool, list[tuple[int, Any]], list[str]]:\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Enhanced verify_lite with match quality validation.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    \\n    issues = []\\n    agent_assignments = []\\n    \\n    for i, subgoal in enumerate(decomposition[\\\"subgoals\\\"]):\\n        match_quality = subgoal.get(\\\"match_quality\\\", \\\"acceptable\\\")\\n        assigned_agent = subgoal.get(\\\"assigned_agent\\\", \\\"\\\")\\n        ideal_agent = subgoal.get(\\\"ideal_agent\\\", \\\"\\\")\\n        \\n        # Validate match_quality makes sense\\n        if match_quality == \\\"excellent\\\" and ideal_agent != assigned_agent:\\n            # LLM said excellent but agents differ - downgrade to acceptable\\n            match_quality = \\\"acceptable\\\"\\n            issues.append(f\\\"Subgoal {i}: Downgraded to acceptable (ideal != assigned)\\\")\\n        \\n        if match_quality == \\\"insufficient\\\":\\n            # Check if we actually have a capable agent the LLM missed\\n            score = _score_agent_capability(assigned_agent, subgoal[\\\"description\\\"])\\n            if score >= 0.5:\\n                match_quality = \\\"acceptable\\\"\\n                issues.append(f\\\"Subgoal {i}: Upgraded to acceptable (capable agent found)\\\")\\n        \\n        # Apply fallback strategy for insufficient\\n        if match_quality == \\\"insufficient\\\":\\n            fallback, reason = FallbackStrategy.get_fallback(\\n                subgoal[\\\"description\\\"],\\n                [a.id for a in available_agents]\\n            )\\n            agent_assignments.append((i, fallback, {\\\"fallback_reason\\\": reason}))\\n        else:\\n            agent_assignments.append((i, assigned_agent, {\\\"match_quality\\\": match_quality}))\\n    \\n    return (len(issues) == 0, agent_assignments, issues)\\n```\\n\\n### 6. One-Shot Example Enhancement for Decomposition\\n\\nAdd domain-specific one-shot examples to the decomposition call:\\n\\n```python\\n# In aurora_reasoning/prompts/examples/example_decompositions.json\\n{\\n  \\\"example_decompositions\\\": [\\n    {\\n      \\\"complexity\\\": \\\"MEDIUM\\\",\\n      \\\"query\\\": \\\"Add OAuth2 authentication to the API\\\",\\n      \\\"decomposition\\\": {\\n        \\\"goal\\\": \\\"Implement OAuth2 authentication\\\",\\n        \\\"subgoals\\\": [\\n          {\\n \\\"depends_on\\\": []\\n          },\\n          {\\n            \\\"description\\\": \\\"Implement OAuth2 endpoints and token management\\\",\\n            \\\"ideal_agent\\\": \\\"@security-engineer\\\",\\n            \\\"ideal_agent_desc\\\": \\\"Security and cryptography specialist\\\",\\n            \\\"assigned_agent\\\": \\\"@full-stack-dev\\\",\\n            \\\"match_quality\\\": \\\"acceptable\\\",\\n            \\\"is_critical\\\": true,\\n            \\\"depends_on\\\": [0]\\n          },\\n          {\\n            \\\"description\\\": \\\"Write (spawn or use assigned) | Tiered routing with quality-aware prompts |\\n| **Fallback Strategy** | None (spawn or fail) | Categorized fallback chain |\\n| **LLM Context** | Agent IDs only | Full capabilities + when_to_use |\\n| **One-Shot Examples** | None for agent matching | Domain-specific examples in prompt |\\n| **Validation** | Basic structural | Quality validation with auto-adjustment Richer LLM context for better initial matching\\n2. One-shot examples for consistent quality decisions\\n3. Fallback chains for graceful degradation\\n4. Quality-aware execution routing\\n\",\n          \"data\": {},\n          \"confidence\": 0.85,\n          \"execution_metadata\": {\n            \"duration_ms\": 79689,\n            \"exit_code\": 0,\n            \"spawned\": false,\n            \"termination_reason\": null,\n            \"heartbeat\": {\n              \"event_count\": 6,\n              \"elapsed_s\": 79.68829846382141,\n              \"idle_s\": 0.37604260444641113\n            }\n          },\n          \"error\": null\n        },\n        {\n          \"subgoal_index\": 1,\n          \"agent_id\": \"full-stack-dev\",\n          \"success\": true,\n          \"summary\": \"## Analysis: Agent Capabilities and Gaps in `aur goals` Decomposition\\n\\n### Current Architecture\\n\\n**Flow**: `aur goals` \\u2192 `PlanDecomposer.decompose()` \\u2192 SOAR `decompose_query()` \\u2192 `aurora_reasoning.decompose.decompose_query()` \\u2192 LLM with `DecomposePromptTemplate`\\n\\n### Available Agents (from `~/.claude/agents/`)\\n\\n| Agent ID | Category | Key Capabilities |\\n|----------|----------|------------------|\\n| `full-stack-dev` | eng | Code implementation, debugging, refactoring, story execution |\\n| `holistic-architect` | eng | System design, API design, infrastructure planning, tech selection |\\n| `qa-test-architect` | qa | Quality gates, test architecture, requirements traceability, NFR validation |\\n| `product-manager` | product | PRD creation, product strategy, roadmap planning |\\n| `product-owner` | product | Backlog management, story refinement, acceptance criteria |\\n| `business-analyst` | general | Market research, brainstorming, competitive analysis |\\n| `ux-expert` | general | UI/UX design, wireframes, prototypes |\\n| `scrum-master` | general | Story creation, epic management, agile processes |\\n| `master` | general | General-purpose catch-all |\\n| `orchestrator` | general | Workflow coordination |\\n\\n### Gaps Identified\\n\\n**1.
